data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/microsoft/amp&quot;&gt;Microsoft&rsquo;s&lt;/a&gt; cloud platform &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/azure&quot; data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/azure/amp&quot;&gt;Azure&lt;/a&gt; has introduced a proof-of-authority (PoA) algorithm on its &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/ethereum-price-index&quot;&gt;Ethereum&lt;/a&gt; (ETH) &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/blockchain&quot; data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/blockchain/amp&quot;&gt;blockchain&lt;/a&gt; product, according to a &lt;a href=&quot;https://azure.microsoft.com/en-us/blog/ethereum-proof-of-authority-on-azure/&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;blog post&lt;/a&gt; Aug. 7.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The new Ethereum network algorithm will reportedly allow a &ldquo;more efficient&rdquo; way of building decentralized applications (&lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/dapps&quot; data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/dapps/amp&quot;&gt;DApps&lt;/a&gt;) for private or consortium networks, where &ldquo;all consensus participants are known and reputable.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;In contrast to &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/explained/proof-of-work-explained&quot; data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/proof-of-work-explained/amp&quot;&gt;proof-of-work&lt;/a&gt; (PoW) &mdash; the existing protocol on Azure &mdash; a PoA algorithm is &lt;a href=&quot;https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proof-of-authority&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;based&lt;/a&gt; on the principle of approved identities or validators on a blockchain, and does not require competition in completing the transactions.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The new Ethereum product on Azure is equipped with a number of features to ensure its correct functioning and security, such as an identity leasing system, Parity&rsquo;s web-assembly support, Azure Monitor, and a Governance DApp.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The identity leasing system intends to ensure that while each member possesses &nbsp;&ldquo;redundant consensus nodes,&rdquo; no two nodes can carry the same identity. The system provides identity protection even in the case of virtual machine (VM) or outage, so the new nodes &ldquo;can quickly spin up and resume the previous nodes&rsquo; identities.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Parity&rsquo;s web-assembly support aims to simplify the process of building &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/smart-contracts&quot; data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/smart-contracts/amp&quot;&gt;smart contracts&lt;/a&gt;, enabling customers to write them in languages that are more familiar than the existing Solidity programming language on the ETH blockchain. The blog post notes that developers will now be able to write DApps in such languages as C, C++, and Rust.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The Governance DApp solution intends to simplify voting and validator delegation in the process of participation in a consortium. By enabling this feature, the developers provide customers with a level of &lt;a href=&quot;https://whatis.techtarget.com/definition/abstraction&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;abstraction&lt;/a&gt;, which allows programmers to hide all but the relevant data about an object in order to lessen complexity and boost efficiency.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The Governance DApp will also ensure that each consortium member has control over his or her own keys, which allows for fully protected signing on a user&rsquo;s chosen wallet, the blog post writes.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Microsoft first &lt;a href=&quot;https://azure.microsoft.com/de-de/blog/azure-blockchain-as-a-service-update/&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;announced&lt;/a&gt; the launch of the Ethereum-based Azure cloud computing platform in late 2015. Founded in 2010, Azure provides a global network of Microsoft-managed data centers for developing, testing, deploying, and managing applications and services.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Earlier in June, the &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/r3&quot; data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/r3/amp&quot;&gt;R3&lt;/a&gt; blockchain consortium &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/news/banks-and-regulators-complete-kyc-app-test-on-r3-blockchain-platform&quot; data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/banks-and-regulators-complete-kyc-app-test-on-r3-blockchain-platform/amp&quot;&gt;announced&lt;/a&gt; that the firm &mdash; together with 39 global financial companies &mdash; had successfully tested its know your customer (&lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/kyc&quot; data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/kyc/amp&quot;&gt;KYC&lt;/a&gt;) application, running a total of 45 nodes on Microsoft Azure.&lt;/p&gt; \" v-on:change-post-visibility=\"changePostVisibility\"> <div :data-post-id=\"post.id\" class=\"post-area\" v-observe-visibility=\"visibilityChanged\"> <div class=\"post-header\"> <div datetime=\"2018-08-08t18:16:00+01:00\" class=\"date\">21 HOURS AGO</div> <div class=\"staff\"> <div class=\"user\"> <div class=\"avatar\" style=\"background-image: url('https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/150_Ly9jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy84NmZhZWYyMGQzMGZjNzM5MTY5ZWVkZWJkM2Q1Njk4OS5qcGc=.jpg');\"></div> <div class=\"role\">By </div> <div class=\"name\"> <a href=\"#\" data-hash=\"true\" data-link=\"aHR0cHM6Ly9jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9hdXRob3JzL2hlbGVuX3BhcnR6\" target=\"_self\">Helen Partz</a> </div> </div> </div> <h1 class=\"header\">Microsoft Introduces Ethereum Proof-of-Authority Algorithm on Azure</h1> <p class=\"post-description\">Microsoft Azure has introduced a proof-of-authority algorithm on its Ethereum-based cloud computing platform.</p> </div> <div class=\"referral_widget\"> <div class=\"referral_stats total-views\"> <span class=\"item views_s\"></span> <span class=\"total-qty\">19111</span> <span class=\"views\">Total views</span> </div> <div class=\"referral_stats total-shares\"> <span class=\"total-qty\">517</span> <span class=\"views\">Total shares</span> </div> </div> <div class=\"post-content\"> <div class=\"image\"> <img srcset=\"https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/740_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy9hOTcxMTdmYjhkNTYzOGIxOTY0N2VlYThiMTU1MjE2Ny5qcGc=.jpg 1x, https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/1480_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy9hOTcxMTdmYjhkNTYzOGIxOTY0N2VlYThiMTU1MjE2Ny5qcGc=.jpg 2x\" src=\"https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/740_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy9hOTcxMTdmYjhkNTYzOGIxOTY0N2VlYThiMTU1MjE2Ny5qcGc=.jpg\" alt=\"Microsoft Introduces Ethereum Proof-of-Authority Algorithm on Azure\"/> <p class='sponsored badge badge-default'>News</p> </div> <div class=\"post-full-text contents js-post-full-text\" itemprop=\"articleBody\"><p dir=\"ltr\"><a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/microsoft\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/microsoft/amp\">Microsoft&rsquo;s</a> cloud platform <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/azure\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/azure/amp\">Azure</a> has introduced a proof-of-authority (PoA) algorithm on its <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/ethereum-price-index\">Ethereum</a> (ETH) <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/blockchain\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/blockchain/amp\">blockchain</a> product, according to a <a href=\"https://azure.microsoft.com/en-us/blog/ethereum-proof-of-authority-on-azure/\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">blog post</a> Aug. 7.</p> <p>The new Ethereum network algorithm will reportedly allow a &ldquo;more efficient&rdquo; way of building decentralized applications (<a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/dapps\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/dapps/amp\">DApps</a>) for private or consortium networks, where &ldquo;all consensus participants are known and reputable.&rdquo;</p> <p>In contrast to <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/explained/proof-of-work-explained\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/proof-of-work-explained/amp\">proof-of-work</a> (PoW) &mdash; the existing protocol on Azure &mdash; a PoA algorithm is <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proof-of-authority\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">based</a> on the principle of approved identities or validators on a blockchain, and does not require competition in completing the transactions.</p> <p>The new Ethereum product on Azure is equipped with a number of features to ensure its correct functioning and security, such as an identity leasing system, Parity&rsquo;s web-assembly support, Azure Monitor, and a Governance DApp.</p> <p>The identity leasing system intends to ensure that while each member possesses &nbsp;&ldquo;redundant consensus nodes,&rdquo; no two nodes can carry the same identity. The system provides identity protection even in the case of virtual machine (VM) or outage, so the new nodes &ldquo;can quickly spin up and resume the previous nodes&rsquo; identities.&rdquo;</p> <p>Parity&rsquo;s web-assembly support aims to simplify the process of building <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/smart-contracts\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/smart-contracts/amp\">smart contracts</a>, enabling customers to write them in languages that are more familiar than the existing Solidity programming language on the ETH blockchain. The blog post notes that developers will now be able to write DApps in such languages as C, C++, and Rust.</p> <p>The Governance DApp solution intends to simplify voting and validator delegation in the process of participation in a consortium. By enabling this feature, the developers provide customers with a level of <a href=\"https://whatis.techtarget.com/definition/abstraction\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">abstraction</a>, which allows programmers to hide all but the relevant data about an object in order to lessen complexity and boost efficiency.</p> <p>The Governance DApp will also ensure that each consortium member has control over his or her own keys, which allows for fully protected signing on a user&rsquo;s chosen wallet, the blog post writes.</p> <p>Microsoft first <a href=\"https://azure.microsoft.com/de-de/blog/azure-blockchain-as-a-service-update/\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">announced</a> the launch of the Ethereum-based Azure cloud computing platform in late 2015. Founded in 2010, Azure provides a global network of Microsoft-managed data centers for developing, testing, deploying, and managing applications and services.</p> <p>Earlier in June, the <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/r3\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/r3/amp\">R3</a> blockchain consortium <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/news/banks-and-regulators-complete-kyc-app-test-on-r3-blockchain-platform\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/banks-and-regulators-complete-kyc-app-test-on-r3-blockchain-platform/amp\">announced</a> that the firm &mdash; together with 39 global financial companies &mdash; had successfully tested its know your customer (<a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/kyc\" data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/kyc/amp\">KYC</a>) application, running a total of 45 nodes on Microsoft Azure.</p> </div> <post-subscribe Hawley will go on to face to Democratic Missouri Sen. Claire McCaskill in the general election. Petersen &lt;a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/AP4Liberty/status/1027025637788344321?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw%7Ctwcamp%5Etweetembed%7Ctwterm%5E1027025637788344321&amp;ref_url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ccn.com%2Fbitcoin-friendly-u-s-senate-candidate-austin-petersen-loses-republican-primary%2F&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;tweeted:&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;blockquote&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&ldquo;Sorry I couldn&#039;t pull out a win for us, friends. My faults as a candidate are my own, and not the fault of our activists. I am not a perfect messenger. One day soon I believe we will see more leaders who rise up and fight for our cause more fiercely and more successfully than I.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/blockquote&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;In February, ABC News &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://abcnews-go-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/abcnews.go.com/amp/Politics/bitcoin-popular-political-campaign-donations/story?id=52873921&quot; href=&quot;https://abcnews.go.com/Politics/bitcoin-popular-political-campaign-donations/story?id=52873921&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;reported&lt;/a&gt; that Petersen&rsquo;s campaign for Senate received 24 donations in Bitcoin amounting to just under $10,000 total. One such donation was reportedly the largest BTC donation ever received in a federal election.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;Upon the receipt on Dec. 20, the &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/bitcoin-for-america-cryptocurrencies-in-campaign-finance/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/news/bitcoin-for-america-cryptocurrencies-in-campaign-finance&quot;&gt;contribution&lt;/a&gt; of 0.284 BTC was purportedly converted to U.S. dollars. At the time the donation was worth over $4,500, putting the donation over the Federal election limit of $2,700 per individual. The candidate&rsquo;s &lt;a href=&quot;https://bitpay.com/247436/donate&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;website&lt;/a&gt; explained that the first $2,700 would go toward activities in the primary election, while the remaining amount would be used in the general election. Petersen&rsquo;s campaign manager Jeff Carson said on his behalf:&lt;/p&gt; &lt;blockquote&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&quot;I think it goes without saying we&#039;re going to see a lot more of [cryptocurrency] in terms of campaign contributions and campaign financing... Austin is personally a fan of competition in the marketplace, even when it comes to our currency. With the rise of cryptocurrencies like Bitcoin, it was a no brainer for us to use those.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/blockquote&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;Petersen&rsquo;s campaign represented an opportunity for crypto advocates to have a lawmaker on their side on Capitol Hill, as &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/us-lawmaker-calls-for-more-action-from-congress-on-regulating-crypto/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/news/us-lawmaker-calls-for-more-action-from-congress-on-regulating-crypto&quot;&gt;some members&lt;/a&gt; of Congress call for increased control and others &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/us-sec-official-says-ico-regulation-should-be-balanced-congressman-suggests-ban/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/news/us-sec-official-says-ico-regulation-should-be-balanced-congressman-suggests-ban&quot;&gt;characterize crypto outright&lt;/a&gt; as a refuge for &ldquo;charlatans and scammers.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;Some American lawmakers are taking a more tempered approach to digital currencies, even becoming hodlers themselves. Earlier this week, Cointelegraph &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/us-chair-of-house-judiciary-committee-discloses-ownership-of-cryptocurrency/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/news/us-chair-of-house-judiciary-committee-discloses-ownership-of-cryptocurrency&quot;&gt;reported&lt;/a&gt; that the Chair of the Judiciary Committee of the &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/usa/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/usa&quot;&gt;U.S.&lt;/a&gt; House of Representatives revealed that he has holdings in Bitcoin, Ethereum (&lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/ethereum-price-index&quot;&gt;ETH&lt;/a&gt;), and Bitcoin Cash (&lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/bitcoin-cash/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/bitcoin-cash&quot;&gt;BCH&lt;/a&gt;). Congressman Bob Goodlatte (R-VA) reported that he owns between $17,000 and $80,000 in crypto on his mandatory annual Financial Disclosure Statement.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Meanwhile, Libertarian Party candidate for Wisconsin governor Phil Anderson &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/libertarian-party-gubernatorial-campaign-to-accept-btc-despite-unclear-legal-framework/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/news/libertarian-party-gubernatorial-campaign-to-accept-btc-despite-unclear-legal-framework&quot;&gt;said&lt;/a&gt; in July that he will accept BTC donations despite the state&rsquo;s Ethics Commission&rsquo;s finding them a &ldquo;serious challenge&rdquo; to compliance with state law. Anderson stated that &nbsp;his decision to accept BTC does not mean his party is &ldquo;thumbing [their] noses at the [commission],&rdquo; as he believes they are abiding by the law.&lt;/p&gt; \" v-on:change-post-visibility=\"changePostVisibility\"> <div :data-post-id=\"post.id\" class=\"post-area\" v-observe-visibility=\"visibilityChanged\"> <div class=\"post-header\"> <div datetime=\"2018-08-09t01:37:00+01:00\" class=\"date\">13 HOURS AGO</div> <div class=\"staff\"> <div class=\"user\"> <div class=\"avatar\" style=\"background-image: url('/assets/img/icons/author_female.png');\"></div> <div class=\"role\">By </div> <div class=\"name\"> <a href=\"#\" data-hash=\"true\" data-link=\"aHR0cHM6Ly9jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9hdXRob3JzL2FuYS1hbGV4YW5kcmU=\" target=\"_self\">Ana Alexandre</a> </div> </div> </div> <h1 class=\"header\">Bitcoin-Friendly US Senate Candidate Defeated in Republican Primary Elections</h1> <p class=\"post-description\">A pro-Bitcoin U.S. Senate candidate, Austin Petersen, lost the Republican primary election in the state of Missouri.</p> </div> <div class=\"referral_widget\"> <div class=\"referral_stats total-views\"> <span class=\"item views_s\"></span> <span class=\"total-qty\">10254</span> <span class=\"views\">Total views</span> </div> <div class=\"referral_stats total-shares\"> <span class=\"total-qty\">210</span> <span class=\"views\">Total shares</span> </div> </div> <div class=\"post-content\"> <div class=\"image\"> <img srcset=\"https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/740_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy9mMDJhNzEwZWQyN2Y0MjZiNzdlZGI1NWJjMjZkYTk1NS5qcGc=.jpg 1x, https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/1480_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy9mMDJhNzEwZWQyN2Y0MjZiNzdlZGI1NWJjMjZkYTk1NS5qcGc=.jpg 2x\" src=\"https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/740_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy9mMDJhNzEwZWQyN2Y0MjZiNzdlZGI1NWJjMjZkYTk1NS5qcGc=.jpg\" alt=\"Bitcoin-Friendly US Senate Candidate Defeated in Republican Primary Elections\"/> <p class='sponsored badge badge-default'>News</p> </div> <div class=\"post-full-text contents js-post-full-text\" itemprop=\"articleBody\"><p dir=\"ltr\">U.S. Senate candidate Austin Petersen, who is known for his Bitcoin (<a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/bitcoin-price-index\">BTC</a>) advocacy, lost the Republican <a href=\"http://enr.sos.mo.gov/\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">primary election</a> Aug. 7.</p> <p dir=\"ltr\">According to unofficial results published by the Missouri Secretary of State, Petersen lost the battle to Attorney General Josh Hawley, who received 58.6 percent of the 663,553 votes. Hawley will go on to face to Democratic Missouri Sen. Claire McCaskill in the general election. Petersen <a href=\"https://twitter.com/AP4Liberty/status/1027025637788344321?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw%7Ctwcamp%5Etweetembed%7Ctwterm%5E1027025637788344321&amp;ref_url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ccn.com%2Fbitcoin-friendly-u-s-senate-candidate-austin-petersen-loses-republican-primary%2F\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">tweeted:</a></p> <blockquote> <p dir=\"ltr\">&ldquo;Sorry I couldn't pull out a win for us, friends. My faults as a candidate are my own, and not the fault of our activists. I am not a perfect messenger. One day soon I believe we will see more leaders who rise up and fight for our cause more fiercely and more successfully than I.&rdquo;</p> </blockquote> <p dir=\"ltr\">In February, ABC News <a data-amp=\"https://abcnews-go-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/abcnews.go.com/amp/Politics/bitcoin-popular-political-campaign-donations/story?id=52873921\" href=\"https://abcnews.go.com/Politics/bitcoin-popular-political-campaign-donations/story?id=52873921\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">reported</a> that Petersen&rsquo;s campaign for Senate received 24 donations in Bitcoin amounting to just under $10,000 total. One such donation was reportedly the largest BTC donation ever received in a federal election.</p> <p dir=\"ltr\">Upon the receipt on Dec. 20, the <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/bitcoin-for-america-cryptocurrencies-in-campaign-finance/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/news/bitcoin-for-america-cryptocurrencies-in-campaign-finance\">contribution</a> of 0.284 BTC was purportedly converted to U.S. dollars. At the time the donation was worth over $4,500, putting the donation over the Federal election limit of $2,700 per individual. The candidate&rsquo;s <a href=\"https://bitpay.com/247436/donate\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">website</a> explained that the first $2,700 would go toward activities in the primary election, while the remaining amount would be used in the general election. Petersen&rsquo;s campaign manager Jeff Carson said on his behalf:</p> <blockquote> <p dir=\"ltr\">\"I think it goes without saying we're going to see a lot more of [cryptocurrency] in terms of campaign contributions and campaign financing... Austin is personally a fan of competition in the marketplace, even when it comes to our currency. With the rise of cryptocurrencies like Bitcoin, it was a no brainer for us to use those.\"</p> </blockquote> <p dir=\"ltr\">Petersen&rsquo;s campaign represented an opportunity for crypto advocates to have a lawmaker on their side on Capitol Hill, as <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/us-lawmaker-calls-for-more-action-from-congress-on-regulating-crypto/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/news/us-lawmaker-calls-for-more-action-from-congress-on-regulating-crypto\">some members</a> of Congress call for increased control and others <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/us-sec-official-says-ico-regulation-should-be-balanced-congressman-suggests-ban/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/news/us-sec-official-says-ico-regulation-should-be-balanced-congressman-suggests-ban\">characterize crypto outright</a> as a refuge for &ldquo;charlatans and scammers.&rdquo;</p> <p dir=\"ltr\">Some American lawmakers are taking a more tempered approach to digital currencies, even becoming hodlers themselves. Earlier this week, Cointelegraph <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/us-chair-of-house-judiciary-committee-discloses-ownership-of-cryptocurrency/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/news/us-chair-of-house-judiciary-committee-discloses-ownership-of-cryptocurrency\">reported</a> that the Chair of the Judiciary Committee of the <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/usa/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/usa\">U.S.</a> House of Representatives revealed that he has holdings in Bitcoin, Ethereum (<a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/ethereum-price-index\">ETH</a>), and Bitcoin Cash (<a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/bitcoin-cash/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/bitcoin-cash\">BCH</a>). Congressman Bob Goodlatte (R-VA) reported that he owns between $17,000 and $80,000 in crypto on his mandatory annual Financial Disclosure Statement.</p> <p>Meanwhile, Libertarian Party candidate for Wisconsin governor Phil Anderson <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/news/libertarian-party-gubernatorial-campaign-to-accept-btc-despite-unclear-legal-framework/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/news/libertarian-party-gubernatorial-campaign-to-accept-btc-despite-unclear-legal-framework\">said</a> in July that he will accept BTC donations despite the state&rsquo;s Ethics Commission&rsquo;s finding them a &ldquo;serious challenge&rdquo; to compliance with state law. Anderson stated that &nbsp;his decision to accept BTC does not mean his party is &ldquo;thumbing [their] noses at the [commission],&rdquo; as he believes they are abiding by the law.</p> </div> rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;paper&lt;/a&gt;, the authors intend to provide a &ldquo;risk-return tradeoff&rdquo; of major cryptocurrencies such as &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/bitcoin-price-index&quot;&gt;Bitcoin&lt;/a&gt; (BTC), &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/ethereum-price-index&quot;&gt;Ethereum&lt;/a&gt; (ETH), and &lt;a href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/xrp-price-index&quot;&gt;Ripple&lt;/a&gt; (XRP), according to its historical performance data.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;The experts &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://www-cnbc-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/www.cnbc.com/amp/2018/08/08/yale-economists-share-strategy-for-buying-bitcoin-ripple-ethereum.html&quot; href=&quot;https://www.cnbc.com/2018/08/08/yale-economists-share-strategy-for-buying-bitcoin-ripple-ethereum.html&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;reportedly&lt;/a&gt; analyzed the behavior of Bitcoin between 2011 and 2018, while Ripple and Ethereum data was tracked since their inceptions in &lt;a href=&quot;https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ripple_(payment_protocol)&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow,noopener&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;2012&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/ethereum/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/ethereum&quot;&gt;2015&lt;/a&gt;, respectively.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;In the study, Tsyvinski and Liu found that cryptocurrencies &ldquo;have no exposure&rdquo; to most common &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/stocks/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/stocks&quot;&gt;stock&lt;/a&gt; markets, as well as to returns of currencies and commodities and macroeconomic factors. Instead, the researchers assert that &ldquo;cryptocurrency returns can be predicted by factors which are specific to cryptocurrency markets.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;Among these factors is a &ldquo;strong time-series momentum effect.&rdquo; Tsyvinski and Liu argue that if the price of Bitcoin increases over a week, it is likely keep growing over the following week. The researchers note that a sharp increase of Bitcoin&rsquo;s price stimulates higher demand in the market, which leads to bigger &lt;a data-amp=&quot;https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/investments/amp&quot; href=&quot;https://cointelegraph.com/tags/investments&quot;&gt;investments&lt;/a&gt;. The study says that the &ldquo;momentum effect was stronger&rdquo; for Bitcoin, but was &ldquo;still statistically significant&rdquo; with Ethereum and Ripple.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Apart from the momentum effect, the Yale researchers mention the factor of investor attention, which is a correlation between crypto prices and the number of posts and queries for cryptocurrencies on social media and in search engines. Ultimately, Tsyvinski states:&lt;/p&gt; &lt;blockquote&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;All things can happen. Maybe the statistical patterns that we find are going to completely change. Maybe tomorrow Bitcoin is going to be prohibited by regulators, maybe it&#039;s going to be completely hacked, there are many things one would take into account.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/blockquote&gt; \" v-on:change-post-visibility=\"changePostVisibility\"> <div :data-post-id=\"post.id\" class=\"post-area\" v-observe-visibility=\"visibilityChanged\"> <div class=\"post-header\"> <div datetime=\"2018-08-08t23:15:00+01:00\" class=\"date\">16 HOURS AGO</div> <div class=\"staff\"> <div class=\"user\"> <div class=\"avatar\" style=\"background-image: url('https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/150_Ly9jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy84NmZhZWYyMGQzMGZjNzM5MTY5ZWVkZWJkM2Q1Njk4OS5qcGc=.jpg');\"></div> <div class=\"role\">By </div> <div class=\"name\"> <a href=\"#\" data-hash=\"true\" data-link=\"aHR0cHM6Ly9jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9hdXRob3JzL2hlbGVuX3BhcnR6\" target=\"_self\">Helen Partz</a> </div> </div> </div> <h1 class=\"header\">Yale Research Proposes Factors for Crypto Price Prediction</h1> <p class=\"post-description\">Yale university financial experts have suggested a system of factors to predict price trends in major cryptocurrencies.</p> </div> <div class=\"referral_widget\"> <div class=\"referral_stats total-views\"> <span class=\"item views_s\"></span> <span class=\"total-qty\">19723</span> <span class=\"views\">Total views</span> </div> <div class=\"referral_stats total-shares\"> <span class=\"total-qty\">263</span> <span class=\"views\">Total shares</span> </div> </div> <div class=\"post-content\"> <div class=\"image\"> <img srcset=\"https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/740_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy85ZDEzMDY4OWI5ODgwNWI0ODQ3YWRkMzU2NjQ1OWYwYy5qcGc=.jpg 1x, https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/1480_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy85ZDEzMDY4OWI5ODgwNWI0ODQ3YWRkMzU2NjQ1OWYwYy5qcGc=.jpg 2x\" src=\"https://images.cointelegraph.com/images/740_aHR0cHM6Ly9zMy5jb2ludGVsZWdyYXBoLmNvbS9zdG9yYWdlL3VwbG9hZHMvdmlldy85ZDEzMDY4OWI5ODgwNWI0ODQ3YWRkMzU2NjQ1OWYwYy5qcGc=.jpg\" alt=\"Yale Research Proposes Factors for Crypto Price Prediction\"/> <p class='sponsored badge badge-default'>News</p> </div> <div class=\"post-full-text contents js-post-full-text\" itemprop=\"articleBody\"><p dir=\"ltr\">Yale University financial experts have suggested a system of factors to <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/predictions/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/predictions\">predict</a> price trends in major <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/cryptocurrencies/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/cryptocurrencies\">cryptocurrencies</a>, according to an <a href=\"https://news.yale.edu/2018/08/06/assessing-cryptocurrency-yale-economist-aleh-tsyvinski\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">official statement</a> by YaleNews Aug. 6.</p> <p dir=\"ltr\">The new study was conducted by Yale economist Aleh Tsyvinski and Yukun Liu, a Ph.D. candidate in the Department of Economics, and is reportedly the &ldquo;first-ever comprehensive economic analysis of cryptocurrency and the <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/blockchain/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/blockchain\">blockchain</a> technology.&rdquo;</p> <p dir=\"ltr\">In the <a href=\"http://www.nber.org/papers/w24877\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">paper</a>, the authors intend to provide a &ldquo;risk-return tradeoff&rdquo; of major cryptocurrencies such as <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/bitcoin-price-index\">Bitcoin</a> (BTC), <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/ethereum-price-index\">Ethereum</a> (ETH), and <a href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/xrp-price-index\">Ripple</a> (XRP), according to its historical performance data.</p> <p dir=\"ltr\">The experts <a data-amp=\"https://www-cnbc-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/www.cnbc.com/amp/2018/08/08/yale-economists-share-strategy-for-buying-bitcoin-ripple-ethereum.html\" href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/2018/08/08/yale-economists-share-strategy-for-buying-bitcoin-ripple-ethereum.html\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">reportedly</a> analyzed the behavior of Bitcoin between 2011 and 2018, while Ripple and Ethereum data was tracked since their inceptions in <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ripple_(payment_protocol)\" rel=\"nofollow,noopener\" target=\"_blank\">2012</a> and <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/ethereum/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/ethereum\">2015</a>, respectively.</p> <p dir=\"ltr\">In the study, Tsyvinski and Liu found that cryptocurrencies &ldquo;have no exposure&rdquo; to most common <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/stocks/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/stocks\">stock</a> markets, as well as to returns of currencies and commodities and macroeconomic factors. Instead, the researchers assert that &ldquo;cryptocurrency returns can be predicted by factors which are specific to cryptocurrency markets.&rdquo;</p> <p dir=\"ltr\">Among these factors is a &ldquo;strong time-series momentum effect.&rdquo; Tsyvinski and Liu argue that if the price of Bitcoin increases over a week, it is likely keep growing over the following week. The researchers note that a sharp increase of Bitcoin&rsquo;s price stimulates higher demand in the market, which leads to bigger <a data-amp=\"https://cointelegraph-com.cdn.ampproject.org/c/s/cointelegraph.com/tags/investments/amp\" href=\"https://cointelegraph.com/tags/investments\">investments</a>. The study says that the &ldquo;momentum effect was stronger&rdquo; for Bitcoin, but was &ldquo;still statistically significant&rdquo; with Ethereum and Ripple.</p> <p>Apart from the momentum effect, the Yale researchers mention the factor of investor attention, which is a correlation between crypto prices and the number of posts and queries for cryptocurrencies on social media and in search engines. Ultimately, Tsyvinski states:</p> <blockquote> <p>\"All things can happen. Maybe the statistical patterns that we find are going to completely change. Maybe tomorrow Bitcoin is going to be prohibited by regulators, maybe it's going to be completely hacked, there are many things one would take into account.\"</p> </blockquote> </div> <post-subscribe
